20#include <dlfcn.h>
21#include <gconv.h>
22#include <stdint.h>

24/*
25 * This module does conversions between gb2312 and big5 encodings.
26 * It is necessary because gb2312 encoding use simplified chinese,
27 * while big5 use traditional one. Often times both the simplified
28 * version of a chinese character and its traditional counterpart
29 * are presented in unicode and have distinctive code values. So
30 * an indirect method through UCS4 (GB2312 <=> UCS4 <=> BIG5) will
31 * not do the work correctly.
32 *
33 * --- Yong Li <rigel863@yahoo.com>
34 */
35
36

4768 [0x363f] = "\xda\xdd", [0x3644] = "\xf2\xa8", [0x3645] = "\xc8\xa7",
4769 [0x3649] = "\xe6\xf8", [0x364d] = "\xf0\xb5", [0x3650] = "\xed\xb0",
4770 [0x3651] = "\xe8\xf9", [0x365a] = "\xe3\xce", [0x3664] = "\xf6\xe2",
4771 [0x3665] = "\xf0\xbf", [0x3666] = "\xe4\xd9", [0x366c] = "\xc6\xe5",
4772 [0x366d] = "\xd0\xe2", [0x366e] = "\xc0\xef", [0x366f] = "\xc7\xbd",
4773 [0x3670] = "\xba\xe3", [0x3671] = "\xd7\xb1",
4774};
4775
4776
4777/* Definitions used in the body of the `gconv' function. */
4778#define CHARSET_NAME "EUC-CN//"
4779#define FROM_LOOP from_gb2312_to_big5
4780#define TO_LOOP from_big5_to_gb2312
4781#define DEFINE_INIT 1
4782#define DEFINE_FINI 1
4783#define MIN_NEEDED_FROM 1
4784#define MAX_NEEDED_FROM 2
4785#define MIN_NEEDED_TO 1
4786#define MAX_NEEDED_TO 2
4787#define ONE_DIRECTION 0
4788
4789
4790/* First define the conversion function from GB2312 to BIG5. */
4791#define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT MIN_NEEDED_FROM
4792#define MAX_NEEDED_INPUT MAX_NEEDED_FROM
4793#define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT MIN_NEEDED_TO
4794#define MAX_NEEDED_OUTPUT MAX_NEEDED_TO
4795#define LOOPFCT FROM_LOOP
4796#define BODY \
4797 { \
4798 uint32_t ch = *inptr; \
4799 \
4800 if (ch <= 0x7f) \
4801 *outptr++ = *inptr++; \
4802 else if (ch >= 0xa1 && ch <= 0xf7) \
4803 { \
4804 /* Two-byte character. First test whether the \
4805 next byte is also available. */ \
4806 const char *cp; \
4807 int idx; \
4808 \
4809 if (__glibc_unlikely (inptr + 1 >= inend)) \
4810 { \
4811 /* The second character is not available. Store \
4812 the intermediate result. */ \
4813 result = __GCONV_INCOMPLETE_INPUT; \
4814 break; \
4815 } \
4816 \
4817 idx = (ch - 0xa1) * 94; \
4818 ch = inptr[1]; \
4819 \
4820 /* All second bytes of a multibyte character must be >= 0xa1. */ \
4821 if (__glibc_unlikely (ch < 0xa1)) \
4822 { \
4823 /* This is an illegal character. */ \
4824 STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1); \
4825 } \
4826 \
4827 idx += ch - 0xa1; \
4828 \
4829 /* Get the value from the table. */ \
4830 cp = __from_gb2312_to_big5[idx]; \
4831 if (__glibc_unlikely (cp[0] == '\0')) \
4832 { \
4833 /* We do not have a mapping for this character. \
4834 If ignore errors, map it to 0xa1bc - big5 box character */ \
4835 result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT; \
4836 if (! ignore_errors_p ()) \
4837 break; \
4838 \
4839 /* See if there is enough room to write the second byte. */ \
4840 if (__glibc_unlikely (outptr + 1 >= outend)) \
4841 { \
4842 result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT; \
4843 break; \
4844 } \
4845 \
4846 *outptr++ = '\xa1'; \
4847 *outptr++ = '\xbc'; \
4848 inptr += 2; \
4849 ++*irreversible; \
4850 continue; \
4851 } \
4852 else \
4853 { \
4854 /* See whether there is enough room to write the second byte. */ \
4855 if (__builtin_expect (cp[1], '\1') != '\0' \
4856 && __builtin_expect (outptr + 1 >= outend, 0)) \
4857 { \
4858 /* We do not have enough room. */ \
4859 result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT; \
4860 break; \
4861 } \
4862 \
4863 *outptr++ = cp[0]; \
4864 if (cp[1] != '\0') \
4865 *outptr++ = cp[1]; \
4866 } \
4867 \
4868 inptr += 2; \
4869 } \
4870 else \
4871 { \
4872 /* This is illegal. */ \
4873 STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1); \
4874 } \
4875 }
4876#define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
4877#include <iconv/loop.c>
4878
4879/* Next, define the other direction. */
4880#define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT MIN_NEEDED_TO
4881#define MAX_NEEDED_INPUT MAX_NEEDED_TO
4882#define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT MIN_NEEDED_FROM
4883#define MAX_NEEDED_OUTPUT MAX_NEEDED_FROM
4884#define LOOPFCT TO_LOOP
4885#define BODY \
4886 { \
4887 uint32_t ch = *inptr; \
4888 \
4889 if (ch <= 0x7f) \
4890 *outptr++ = *inptr++; \
4891 else if (ch >= 0xa1 && ch <= 0xf9) \
4892 { \
4893 /* Two byte character. First test whether the \
4894 next byte is also available. */ \
4895 const char *cp; \
4896 int idx; \
4897 \
4898 if (__glibc_unlikely (inptr + 1 >= inend)) \
4899 { \
4900 /* The second character is not available. Store \
4901 the intermediate result. */ \
4902 result = __GCONV_INCOMPLETE_INPUT; \
4903 break; \
4904 } \
4905 \
4906 idx = (ch - 0xa1) * 157; \
4907 ch = inptr[1]; \
4908 /* See if the second byte is in the correct range. */ \
4909 if (ch >= 0x40 && ch <= 0x7e) \
4910 idx += ch - 0x40; \
4911 else if (__builtin_expect (ch >= 0xa1, 1) \
4912 && __builtin_expect (ch <= 0xfe, 1)) \
4913 idx += 0x3f + (ch - 0xa1); \
4914 else \
4915 { \
4916 /* This is an illegal character. */ \
4917 STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1); \
4918 } \
4919 \
4920 /* Get the value from the table. */ \
4921 cp = __from_big5_to_gb2312 [idx]; \
4922 if (__glibc_unlikely (cp[0] == '\0')) \
4923 { \
4924 /* We do not have a mapping for this character. \
4925 If ignore errors, map it to 0xa1f5 - gb box character */ \
4926 result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT; \
4927 if (! ignore_errors_p ()) \
4928 break; \
4929 \
4930 /* See if there is enough room to write the second byte. */ \
4931 if (__glibc_unlikely (outptr + 1 >= outend)) \
4932 { \
4933 result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT; \
4934 break; \
4935 } \
4936 \
4937 *outptr++ = '\xa1'; \
4938 *outptr++ = '\xf5'; \
4939 inptr += 2; \
4940 ++*irreversible; \
4941 continue; \
4942 } \
4943 else \
4944 { \
4945 /* see if there is enough room to write the second byte. */ \
4946 if (__builtin_expect (cp[1], '\1') != '\0' \
4947 && __builtin_expect (outptr + 1 >= outend, 0)) \
4948 { \
4949 /* We do not have enough room. */ \
4950 result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT; \
4951 break; \
4952 } \
4953 \
4954 *outptr++ = cp[0]; \
4955 if (cp[1] != '\0') \
4956 *outptr++ = cp[1]; \
4957 } \
4958 \
4959 inptr += 2; \
4960 } \
4961 else \
4962 { \
4963 /* This is illegal. */ \
4964 STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1); \
4965 } \
4966 }
4967#define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
4968#include <iconv/loop.c>
